Chișinău apartment report
Listings (left) + Leaflet map (right). Click a listing to zoom/highlight the marker; click a marker to jump to the listing.
What you’re seeing: apartments for purchase (source-specific). Sector borders are approximate OSM admin relations. Late-evening busyness is a composite proxy within ~300m: food/drink density + transit density + culture venues + plaza/pedestrian-zone signal + pedestrian-friendly street length.
(filters)
Overlays (100m grid): each square shows OSM POI counts binned into a 100m×100m grid over Chișinău; color intensity is log-scaled density within that grid cell.
Map legend: pin confirmed pin unconfirmed pin mismatch

Agent assessment — property (ad-anchored)

  • No strong seller emphasis could be reliably extracted from the text.

B) Stated vs not stated (be strict):

  • Explicitly stated:
  • Key building/usage details are not clearly specified in the ad text.
  • Not stated:
  • Exact floor level / storey
  • Elevator / lift
  • Outdoor space (balcony/loggia/terrace/garden)
  • Parking / garage availability and terms
  • Energy certificate figures (HWB / fGEE)
  • Tenancy status (vacant vs rented, end date)
  • Furnishing included/excluded

C) Grounded read-between-the-lines:

  • If the pin is not confirmed, treat nearby-amenity context as approximate and verify the exact micro-location.

D) Viewing questions (bring these):

  • Which floor is it on, and is there a working elevator? (If yes: from which level?)
  • What exactly is included in the monthly costs (utilities, maintenance, building admin), and are there any planned increases?
  • Is the apartment vacant on handover, or is there an existing tenancy/occupant?
  • What is included in the sale (furniture/appliances), and what is excluded?
  • Are there upcoming building works (roof/facade/risers) and what is the reserve fund status (if applicable)?
  • If renovation/first-occupancy language is used: what scope is completed and what is still pending? Can you provide a written spec?
  • If parking is mentioned: is it included, optional, or just nearby? What are the terms and costs?
  • Price: €169,950
  • Rooms: 3
  • Area: Chișinău
